###  Sukanen₁

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Sukanen* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  38
* Origin:  finer|joukahainen|fiwikt
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
